Telegram 52

From He Chengjun, Hankou, to all newspapers: I recently replied to Commander-in-Chief Zhang in a telegram, saying: "I have received Dongri's telegram, which is clear in its reasoning and sincere in its intention, reading it again and again, bringing tears to my eyes. I believe that there is no lack of methods to serve the country, but it is essential to be sincere. There is no lack of ways to stop the chaos, but it is essential to understand each other. At this time, survival depends on ending the conflict, as your opinion states. However, since General Bai's telegram was sent, although the arguments have been heated and considered shocking, the central government still focuses on appeasement and sincerity, repeatedly and gently persuading. If General Bai can consider the Party and the country and cherish the national cause, he should wake up immediately, cover up his past mistakes, and untie the knot, which will not harm him in the slightest. However, according to reports, for the past ten days, General Bai's side has been gathering various reactionaries in Xuzhou, daily discussing ideas that are far from reality, unthinkable, and must destroy the overall situation. On the other hand, he has appointed a large number of commanders, attacking Pinghan in segments. Even the five-route troops under my command have been incorporated into the battle sequence without authorization. In terms of courtesy, they secretly mobilize; in terms of stopping the chaos, they first plot rebellion. The debate on small matters should be limited to the benefit of the Party and the country. If seeking to provoke, it is certainly intended to destroy the overall situation and will be abandoned by the people of the country. I have worked with General Bai for a long time and know him well. He has always been prudent and would not do this. But the reason for this is that he is surrounded by all kinds of reactionaries without realizing it. Every time I think about it, I am deeply saddened. Fortunately, Your Excellency advocates justice and maintains peace. The benevolent are admired by all. However, peace must be achieved through proper means. If General Bai can expel the evil elements and meet sincerely, all requests, as long as they do not conflict with Party discipline and national law, the central government can be generous and seek completeness. Judging from past facts, how has the central government treated General Bai, and how has General Bai treated the central government? You also know this well. At this critical juncture, I want to speak out for justice and promote General Bai's reflection, and I can only rely on you. I humbly submit my views and hope to hear your enlightened teachings." Respectfully submitted, He Chengjun.

However, because Zhang has a different position in the Northeast, he ranks the central government alongside Yan, which is his mistake. Although Yan's troops have arrived in Caozhou, a regiment, Lianzhen's three brigades, and a unit in Dezhou, they are really incapable. Because Han Shi's steps have been set, the second step is to issue a telegram to attack Yan, and the third step is to disband the troops in Henan and Shanxi. The central government telegraphed Yan to persuade him to pull back from the brink and cancel his resignation and ominous actions. Yan replied that he has not reached the brink and cannot be pulled back, and there are no ominous actions, and resignation cannot be cancelled. We see that Yan's best policy at this moment is to step down, and the next best is to withdraw his troops back to Shanxi, or he may be able to survive for a while. Otherwise, the situation will become isolated, which is no longer a problem. In short, 70 to 80 percent of the overall situation has turned around. (March 3rd)

Jin Army Stationed in Dezhou 54

Jinan Correspondence: Since the Jin army launched, Shandong has borne the brunt. Commander-in-Chief Jiang has repeatedly ordered the Shandong army to remain calm and not to start a war lightly. Therefore, Chen Tiaoyuan transferred the 2nd Security Brigade of Chen Xiaosi, stationed in Dezhou, to southern Shandong. The Jin army's plainclothes team entered Dezhou at 3 p.m. on March 1. Most of the Shandong army is now in the Yucheng and Pingyuan areas. Heavy troops have been deployed on both the north and south banks of the Yellow River in Shandong. In western Shandong, the 42nd Infantry Division of Feng Pengzhu and the 21st Cavalry Division of the Jin army are successively developing towards Caozhou. As for the remnants of Gao Guizi, after fleeing from Yixian, Linyi, and Anqiu to Zhucheng, the 26th Division of the Central Army and the 46th and 55th Divisions of Shandong are attacking from all sides and will be resolved within days. (March 3rd)

Feng Yuxiang Arrives in Taiyuan 55

Taiyuan Correspondence: The issue of the current situation is gradually being revealed. Since Yan Xishan sent a series of telegrams, the atmosphere in Taiyuan has changed. Regarding military affairs, in addition to the part of Yang Xiaoou stationed in Linfen, which was ordered to go north and stationed in Pinding, yesterday the entire 6th Artillery Regiment stationed in the province was transferred to Tianjin. All the supplies were newly purchased, and the arrangements were extremely luxurious. Famous chefs were also hired to prepare food. Liu Zhi Urges Han Shi to Obey the Central Government 56

▲The Second Route Headquarters issued a telegram to persuade Han Shi

Xuzhou Correspondence: The situation between Xuzhou and Henan has always been eased, and the recent atmosphere is even better. The reason is that Han Fuqu has repeatedly sent letters and telegrams to Liu Zhi and sent representatives Tang Xiang and He Qishen to contact him, expressing obedience to the central government. Shi Yousan also telegraphed Liu to express his obedience to the central government and act in accordance with Han Shi. Liu Zhi then sent telegrams to Han Shi, pointing out the great righteousness and urging him to wake up. Therefore, the situation on both sides is improving day by day. Now, the headquarters has sent Chief of Staff Jiang Bocheng, Transportation Commander Qian Zongze, and Chief of Staff of the Third Route Army Li Shuchun to Bian on the evening of the 1st to contact. Han also sent Ordnance Director Zhang Degong from Bian to Beijing on the 3rd to purchase military materials. There is also good news that passenger cars in Xuzhou and Bian have resumed operation. The following is the original record of the four telegrams that the Second Route Headquarters publicly released from Liu Zhi to Han Shi. The development of the situation between Xuzhou and Henan can be seen in these four telegrams.

▲Hao Telegram: Urgent, Chairman Han Xiangfang of Kaifeng, Commander-in-Chief Shi Hanzhang of Guide, I have not seen each other for a long time, and I always miss you very much. The Party and the country have many troubles, and wars are frequent. The people's livelihood is almost exhausted. Recently, more rumors have been spread, and everyone is frightened. The people are worried and cannot live in peace. We soldiers cannot fulfill our duty to save the country and protect the people. Now that the people are so haggard, we are very sad. After detailed investigation, the reason is that ambitious warlords use their personal power and secretly carry out divisive tactics. Only by sincerely supporting the central government, obeying the government, promoting unity, and realizing peace can the people be relieved of their suffering and the country can be free from the danger of collapse. If you are used by others, indulge in anger for a while, harm your own personality, forget the long history, and eventually become the public enemy of the country and be secretly happy by good people. Both of you are strong in the Party and the country, have long enjoyed a reputation, and have a broad vision and insight into the advantages and disadvantages. I hope you can see through the traitorous plots, obey the central government, join hands, and jointly revolutionize. It is not only the fortune of the Party and the country but also the blessing of the region. Being at the end of love, I dare to speak frankly. I hope you will understand and pray for it. I am now in Xuzhou, close to the barracks, and I hope to be taught from time to time, and I am even more grateful. Your brother, Liu Zhi, bows down.

▲Yang Telegram: Urgent, Chairman Han Xiangfang of Kaifeng, I have respectfully read your telegram. I admire your maintenance of peace. As for the change of county magistrates in southern Henan, it was because during the campaign against Tang, most of the county magistrates were appointed by Tang and helped the rebels, so I presented it to the President for approval and replaced them. Now that the war has ended, I have moved to Xuzhou and have not asked about it for a long time. This is a reply. Your brother, Liu Zhi, bows down.

▲Jing Telegram: Urgent, Commander-in-Chief Han Xiangfang of Kaifeng, and please translate to Commander-in-Chief Shi Hanzhang. Supporting the central government, loyalty and sincerity are gratifying. From now on, we generals will join hands, promote peace, and not only will the people's suffering be relieved, but the foundation of the Party and the country will also be consolidated. Great achievements, the whole country admires. Zhi and you have devoted themselves to the revolution and shared difficulties for a long time. Now, when the Party and the country are in trouble, we need each other even more. I hope to work together, be sincere with each other, be consistent from beginning to end, work together, and complete the revolutionary cause and achieve the success of unity. My humble opinion, I cannot express my thick hope. I hope you will understand. Your brother, Liu Zhi, bows down.

▲Dong Telegram: Urgent, Chairman Han Xiangfang of Kaifeng, Secret, Director Hai passed through Xuzhou and forwarded your letter and described all your intentions. I have listened respectfully to everything. Today, I reread your and Hanzhang's joint telegram, and I see your sincerity in maintaining peace and supporting unity. I am even more admired. Now, rumors are intensifying, and the whole country is panic-stricken. If you want to quell the chaos, the responsibility lies with us. Since you and Commander Hanzhang have vowed loyalty to the central government and your determination is as firm as gold and stone, I hope you will quickly make further proposals and express your opposition to Yan. Then, the prestige will spread and intimidate the rebels. It will be easy to eliminate the rebel party. Please convey this to Commander Hanzhang. The personnel appointed in southern Henan have been registered and will be sent to you for consideration of retention or removal. I will report to you first. Your brother, Liu Zhi, bows down.

It is also reported that Jiang Bocheng and Qian Zongze, who were sent by the central government to Kaifeng for contact, returned to Beijing yesterday (4th) morning with Han's representative Li Shuchun and Shi's representative Qin Jianbin. White Russians in Sanhe Town with Black Borders are Planning Trouble 57

▲Organize troops into two parts

▲Actually want to seize Hulunbuir

▲Black Army's All-Victorious Regiment Rushes to Suppress

Harbin Correspondence, 25th - In Hulunbuir Mongolian Banner, 300 miles northeast of Hailar, there is a small town called Sanhe, which used to be an uncultivated area between Shiwei and Lubin counties. In the past, it was barren and uninhabited. After the Russian Revolution and the Red Party came to power, a general group of White Russian descendants fled into our territory and gathered in Sanhe. They have reproduced to this day, with about 300 families and more than 4,000 people. Heilongjiang province is vast, rich in resources, and has lenient policies, so no one has asked about this group or paid attention to their actions. Gradually, an area of hundreds of miles around has become a White Russian settlement. These people usually maintain their lives by raising livestock and farming. They are still in harmony with our Chinese merchants, and the authorities have sympathized with their surviving from a lost country and treated them with special tolerance as fellow countrymen. Last year, during the Russian rebellion, the Red Russians invaded and burned and slaughtered Sanhe. Afterwards, the White Russians petitioned our authorities for permission to purchase firearms for self-defense. When the Manchurian Sea fell and the defeated soldiers and brave men returned from the front line and passed through the area, they were attacked by these people. People were massacred and bullets were confiscated. Merchants passing through the area to escape were also killed. The total number of Chinese military and civilians killed was no less than several hundred. The party used the weapons obtained to organize the army. The leaders are (Shute Laofu) and (Bate Yefu). They are divided into two teams, each with about 250 people, and are actually preparing for a major operation. A few days ago, they even planned to rob a westbound passenger car and harass the Yakeshi station, peeping at Hailar. Zhao Zhongren, the Hulunbuir commissioner, sent a special commissioner to appease them, but the envoy was killed. The authorities were extremely angry. In addition to urgently telegraphing Liang Zhongjia, the Hailar garrison commander, to send troops to assist in the suppression, they also ordered the entire All-Victorious Regiment of the 2nd Cavalry Brigade to rush to search and suppress on the 24th. On the 25th, the Tu regiment arrived in Yakeshi and transported it to Sanhe by train. The area is more than 100 miles away from Sanhe, and it can be reached in one day and one night. It is expected that heavy troops will attack, and it will not be difficult to pacify it soon.

Resolutions of the Third Plenary Session 58

▲ Proposal on Transferring Disbanded Armed Comrades: Resolution of the Disbandment Conference. Although constrained by feudal thinking,

the greatest aspiration of the people and the most important national construction policy that our party adheres to, following the teachings of the Premier, must be implemented without hesitation. Repeated military actions in recent years to suppress reactionary warlords were also aimed at the early completion of disbandment. Now that the reactionary warlords who hold onto troops for self-defense are gradually being eliminated, all resolutions of the Disbandment Conference can be implemented without difficulty. During the implementation, retired officers and soldiers all have revolutionary histories and should be transferred to all construction undertakings to complete the national revolution. Based on this principle, the specific measures for transferring the work of comrades after disbandment are proposed as follows: (1) Establish large-scale police academies, select healthy and somewhat knowledgeable retired officers, enroll them for one or two years of study, and assign them to serve in various provinces and counties after graduation. (2) Establish gendarmerie training institutions, select retired officers with surveying schools, select retired officers with relatively more knowledge, enroll them for one year, and assign them as assistant land surveyors or road surveyors after graduation. (4) Establish civil engineering personnel training institutes, select retired officers with relatively more knowledge, enroll them, and impart the necessary skills and knowledge for civil engineering, for one year. After graduation, assign them to railway engineering agencies, road engineering agencies, or water conservancy engineering agencies as supervisors and engineers, etc. (5) Each army should take turns hiring teachers with rich agricultural or engineering experience to teach the necessary skills in agriculture or engineering. (6) The government may select retired military officers from farming

Page 10

villages who have slightly poorer academic qualifications but rich experience as commissioners of reclamation areas, assisted by foreign agricultural experts, to engage in reclamation projects, based on industrial plans. (7) Organize Northeast, Northwest, and Southwest border inspection groups.

Proposal on Supporting Comrades and Increasing Construction Efficiency

Our party has come to this day with a long history and relying on the long-term struggle of comrades. Among them, those who sacrificed their lives and became disabled for the party already have regulations for commendation and compensation to rely on, so that the elderly are cared for and the young are nurtured. However, those who have ruined their families, dropped out of school, and become destitute due to their efforts in the revolution are still often overlooked, although they are always in the central government's thoughts. Not only that, but all comrades who have worked hard for the party for a long time, regardless of their age, experience, or knowledge, all possess a revolutionary spirit and a deep belief in the doctrine. At this time when political tutelage has begun and everything is waiting to be managed, all our comrades should do their best to devote themselves to all effective paths, lead the masses, and complete political tutelage. Based on this principle, the Party should, on the one hand, encourage comrades to acquire the skills to support themselves and produce for the country, and on the other hand, it should provide all appropriate opportunities. Some comrades forget their ability to automatically contribute to society and the country and want to rely on the party, making the party exhaust itself in responding to individual requests. This is a major mistake. If the central government sits idly by and watches these countless talented people decline day by day, it would be a great pity. The specific measures for supporting comrades and increasing construction efficiency are proposed as follows: (1) Young comrades who have worked hard in revolutionary work should, from now on, shift from destruction to striving to engage in a practical construction work. In order to develop their will and ability, the central government should pay attention to each person's strengths and give them appropriate opportunities, such as the following: 1. Run education businesses or take on education roles after passing examinations. 2. Go to various places to conduct social and economic surveys. 3. Study and inspect the development of education, politics, and industry in border provinces. 4. Serve as county magistrates or local administrative assistants after passing examinations to prepare for local autonomy. 5. Serve as consuls and embassy staff after passing examinations. (2) If young comrades' abilities are not sufficient to meet the needs of their work, the central government should find ways to train and cultivate them to become useful talents for construction. (3) Encourage writing and translation related to party doctrine and party governance, so that young comrades can all strive to learn. The central government will also set up a special compilation and translation office to recruit such talents, guide their work, and review their achievements. (4) Veteran comrades who have participated in the revolution and have made achievements but currently do not have suitable work, the central government should find ways to recruit them to engage in the following types of work: 1. Compile party history. 2. Compile national history. 3. Inspect administration. 4. Supervise land reclamation. 5. Give speeches on party history. 6. Compile local gazetteers. 7. Send them abroad for inspection. (5) For veteran comrades who have contributed to the revolution but are old and frail and unable to work, the central government should provide them with old-age pensions to reward their merits and instruct them to pay attention to promoting local social undertakings and report their progress to the central government every year.

Negotiations on Foreigners Acquiring Property in Zhejiang Province 59

Regarding the Case of British National Mei Tenggen's Property

When the National Revolutionary Army entered Zhejiang, the local people, because the British doctor Mei Tenggen, under the guise of running the Guangji Hospital Medical School with enthusiasm for charity, had engaged in aggression for many years, accumulated resentment for many years. Provincial government sent officials to take over, and a hospital affairs committee was set up to manage the matter. Private property was handled by a liquidation committee. Later, Tan Xin, the dean of the Guangji Hospital run by Mei Tenggen, repeatedly requested the provincial government to return the Guangji Medical School through the British consul stationed in Ningbo. The Zhejiang University and the Department of Civil Affairs jointly submitted the request to the provincial government committee for decision, which approved the return of the hospital and the medical school. The private property was temporarily managed by the Department of Civil Affairs after the hospital affairs committee and others were closed. Unexpectedly, the missionary Gong Duoma moved into the houses on Ma Shi Street on his own, and Tan Xin also continued to request the return of the houses at Ziyun Cave in West Lake, the cemetery at Jiulimatsu on Lingyin Road, and the houses at Zhi Dafangbo. Finally, the British consul sent a letter requesting the return of all of Mei Tenggen's private property in Hangzhou and Moganshan. Mei Tenggen and others first found ways to return the hospital and the medical school, and then requested the return of private property. The steps of foreign negotiations are truly amazing. This time, the provincial government, in addition to notifying the Ma Shi Street houses and instructing them to submit title deeds, household registers, grain certificates, and other documents for review, the Ziyun Cave houses have scenic relations, the Jiulimatsu cemetery is a missionary cemetery purchased in the name of a private individual, and is in contact with the Anglican Church. The ownership of the Zhi Dafangbo houses is still under investigation. Besides informing the department to submit proof, all of Mei Tenggen's private property in Hangzhou and Moganshan has been repeatedly requested by the British consul, and because the inside story is complicated, it is necessary to investigate in detail and handle it properly. In the middle of last month, the Department of Civil Affairs was ordered to investigate and report in detail. It is now heard that the department has followed the order and submitted the report on the liquidation committee's investigation of private property and the recent detailed investigation. After reviewing the report, Zhang Jingjiang, Chairman of the Provincial Government, stated that although the British consul used the Sino-Japanese Treaty as a basis, saying that Mei Tenggen had property rights, the Sino-Japanese Treaty stipulates that the scope of foreign residence is northeast of Gongchen Bridge, with designated boundaries and charter regulations. Foreigners are not allowed to freely acquire property in other places. It is still planned to reject the British consul's request for the return of all private property outside the concession based on the treaty and the violations of regulations in Mei's property acquisition. This case could have been decided at the previous provincial government meeting according to the case handling procedure, but because Chairman Zhang went to Beijing to attend the Third Plenary Session, it has not yet been reviewed. It is heard that as soon as Zhang and Zhu Jiahua, Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, return to Zhejiang, the reply letter can be issued after it is passed at the meeting.

Local Correspondence 60

Songjiang

Water police arrest bandits and escort them to Songjiang. The first district of the Minhang Water Police Provincial Public Security Team reported that Li Huchen, the third team leader, had arrested bandits Liu Xiaomei and others in Shanghai. After interrogation, they confessed that they had repeatedly committed robbery and kidnapping for ransom in various townships in Songjiang Punan, such as the Cai surname case in Sha Jiutu and the cotton boat robbery of Fang Zhengming in Shanyang. There are still several kidnapping cases. After the district chief learned of the confession, he immediately dispatched Zhang Tiange, an inspector of the headquarters, to lead four patrolmen to escort Liu Xiaomei, Wang Shaodi, Li Shan, and Jin Ada, a suspect in another case, to the county government of this county for trial on the 6th. After hearing the case, Auditor Du ordered them to be imprisoned pending investigation.

Arrest of a suspect in embezzling rice funds. Meng Qiuting, a partner of Yao Hengyuan Rice Store in Xitan, this city, embezzled more than 1,000 yuan of rice funds that the store should have received from various stores in Shanghai last year when he was selling goods in Shanghai. He avoided returning to the store. The store sent people to investigate but failed to find him. The store filed a lawsuit with the county government, and the suspect was arrested and sent to the government for trial on the 6th.

Suzhou

Appeal judgment in the prison riot case. After the prison riot in the third sub-prison of Siqian Street last year, the principal offenders Jiang Yingcheng, Liu Aiqun, Zhou Guangya, Li Hui, Cao Shuming, Wang Yi, Bai Xingmin, and Le Changrui were sent to the local court for investigation and trial. The court concluded the case and sentenced them to imprisonment. Jiang and others declared their dissatisfaction and hired lawyers Yang Keng and Zhang Qingyue to draft a statement and appeal to the High Court. The court opened on the afternoon of yesterday (6th) and pronounced the judgment. Jiang Yingcheng, Liu Aiqun, Zhou Guangya, and Li Hui were each sentenced to one year and two months of imprisonment. Cao Shuming and Wang Yi were each sentenced to one year of imprisonment. Bai Xingmin and Le Changrui were each sentenced to four months of imprisonment.

Counter-revolutionary prisoners escorted to Suzhou. The Shanghai Local Court ordered bailiffs yesterday (6th) to escort nine counter-revolutionary prisoners, Wang Qingfeng, Chen Xinglun, Zhong Jian, Xiao Yuhuai, Jin Huanhui, Zhou He, Zhang Yuqing, Wang Ying, and Hu Wencai, to Suzhou and send them to the High Court. They were then sent to the third sub-prison for custody.

Bail for those involved in the Xin Su Dao Bao case. Wang Zhaojie, the director of Xin Su Dao Bao, and staff members Hua Youwen and Yu Yueyun were arrested by Director Zheng of the County Public Security Bureau for publishing information on the farmer's resistance to rent and sent to the High Court for investigation. The prosecutor's office of the High Court repeatedly summoned those involved for investigation and found that there was no counter-revolutionary behavior. Wang and others applied for bail and were approved. Wang, Hua, and others posted bail yesterday (6th) and were released.

Water police encircle and suppress gangsters in Pudong. Since the towns of Wei Jing Tang and Wu Shen Jing in the county were robbed by gangsters from Pudong on the 21st of last month, the gangsters have all fled to Dianshan Lake. The third district of the Water Public Security ordered the 11th, 14th, and 15th teams to go to suppress them. Unexpectedly, the steamer from Shanghai to Huzhou was robbed by the gang leader Taibao A Xu and his gang at Zuo Cang, and many people were shot and injured. After the bandits robbed the property, they fled to Dianshan Lake again. Gong, the district chief of the third district, in addition to telegraphing Chi, the district chief of the first district of Minhang, to send a team to intercept them, also telegraphed the team leaders of the 11th, 14th, and 15th teams to go and join the team boats in the first district to seize the opportunity to suppress them.

Wuxi

Tragic robbery in Changda Mansion. At about 10 o'clock the night before last, more than ten bandits suddenly came to the home of Shen Xiaodi, a villager from Xia'an, Wujitu, Changda Mansion, under the jurisdiction of the county. They spoke in a northern accent and carried weapons such as pistols, sharp knives, and iron bars. They broke into the house. At that time, the Shen family, young and old, had already fallen asleep. After the bandits entered the house, they took Xiaodi from the bed and forced him to tell them where the silver was hidden. Xiaodi refused. The bandits took off Xiaodi's clothes, tied him with a rope, hung him in the kitchen, beat him with a hoe, and slashed his legs with a sharp knife. Blood flowed like a river, but Xiaodi still did not speak. The bandits then used burning firewood to iron Xiaodi's body, causing his flesh to be blurred and unbearable to look at. Xiaodi's second son, Longbao, seeing this, stepped forward to beg for mercy and was also seized by the bandits, stripped of his clothes, hung up, and beaten, leaving him covered in wounds. The bandits then searched and robbed separately. After two hours, they took the stolen goods and fled. After the incident, it was checked and found that they had been robbed of 30 yuan in cash, two gold rings, and clothing, totaling more than 180 yuan in losses. The Shen family and his son were seriously injured and came to the city yesterday to report to the county and ask for the arrest of the bandits and the recovery of the stolen goods.

Changing the auditor for a confirmed trial. Dong, the auditor of this county, was ordered to be transferred to the Nantong County Court Preparatory Committee. The vacancy was filled by Yang, the auditor of Wujiang County, transferred by the High Court. Since Yang was entrusted with an important case by the Department of Civil Affairs, he could not come to Xicheng. President Lin then changed the order and transferred Yu Jitang, the auditor of Kunshan County, to Xicheng to act as an agent. It is heard that Yu will arrive in the county to take office soon. It is also heard that Lu Ying, the auditor of Wujin County, has been transferred to fill the vacancy in Kunshan.

The commissioner of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce came to Xicheng to investigate. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, in accordance with the resolutions of the Second Plenary Session, sent officials to investigate the domestic labor situation and industrial production in districts to improve them. Yesterday, Kong, the minister, appointed Zhu Shikang, a member of the Regulations Committee and director of the Arbitration Section, Chen Bingyao, the director of the Statistics Section, and Tang Qixian and other investigators, a total of twelve people, together with Lin Jizhi, the director of the Labor Hygiene Section of the Ministry of Health, departed from Beijing to investigate Wuyi first. They arrived in Xixi at about 6:00 p.m. In the evening, they discussed the investigation procedures. It was decided that all investigators would be divided into seven groups to investigate and complete the investigation within one week. It is heard that the task of Lin, the director of the Department of Health, is to focus on the hygiene of factory women and child laborers, such as their living, diet, etc., and to prepare to establish a model industrial hygiene zone, designating factories to conduct various labor hygiene matters on a trial basis.

Jiangyin

The central government comforts Li and Zhu, two party members. Qingyang, Li Zhongdan, Zhu Zhaotong and others have made considerable efforts in party affairs. In the past year, in order to prepare for the security regiment, they went to Shanghai to purchase weapons and were assassinated by bandits. The executive committee of the former county party department submitted the report to the province and then to the central government. According to the regulations for comforting party members, each was given a one-time comfort payment of 500 yuan of the third class, which was issued by the provincial government.

Director Lin of the Education Bureau transferred to the province. Lin Yanming, the director of the Education Bureau, took over the matter on October 17 of last year and has been in office for four months. Due to the tide of education, he was ordered to transfer to the province. The order arrived on the 3rd and ordered County Chief Shen to select someone to temporarily replace him and report three people for review and appointment in accordance with the regulations.

Huangtiangang urgently needs to be dredged. Huangtiangang, outside the north, has not been dredged for many years and is gradually silted up. Previously, there were 301 representatives of 20 industries who submitted a report to the Chamber of Commerce and transferred it to the county for review and dredging. The order stated that it seems feasible to draw boat donations to cover the expenses of dredging Huangtiangang, similar to the method of Taixing County. The Construction Bureau should be ordered to review and respond before submitting it for review and instruction.

The Construction Bureau has no right to change the Chengxi route. The south of the Chengxi Highway has been completed, and the north section has been delayed due to office relations. Previously, Xue Chan and others from Sihe Township believed that the Chengxi Road could save bridges, save public funds, and cultivate wasteland into good fields if it went straight south from Dushan Bridge to the west. Director Li of the Construction Bureau believes that the road line has already been detailed and reported to the Construction Department for review and instruction. There is no such right to change the route. The county is requested to transfer the report to the Construction Department for review and instruction.

Zhenjiang

Expediting land registration. The Department of Finance of Jiangsu Province has previously issued a notice to all counties to handle land registration. The department issued rules and forms and ordered that it be officially held on the 10th of last month. Some have reported their establishment, but there are many that have not reported it. The department believes that the land registration is of great importance and the deadline is only six months. The department telegraphed all counties yesterday to hold it on a specific date and report it immediately.

Delineating afforestation areas. The Provincial Afforestation Movement Committee stipulates that tree planting will be carried out on Beigu Mountain from the 6th to the 11th of this month. In accordance with the resolution of the Provincial Government, the area will be divided into twelve areas, and various agencies, groups, and schools will go to plant trees according to the designated area, date, and number of people. The committee has already notified all sectors yesterday.

Nantong

Using work as relief for the Wanggang tidal disaster. The Wanggang River tide has flooded and caused a disaster. Various sectors have raised relief funds. A total of 1,920 yuan has been raised, together with 5,000 yuan allocated by the provincial government, totaling 6,920 yuan. The embankment will be expanded immediately to provide work as relief.

The chief of the Red Army was arrested and sent to the same place for trial. The Jiangbei Five Counties Anti-Bandit Team divided into several routes to suppress the self-proclaimed Red Army Communists. More than a dozen chiefs, including He Guangyin, have been arrested and sent to the same general headquarters for trial.

Various sectors held a meeting to protect the Jiang'an embankment. The Jiang'an embankment in the southwest of Tongyi has been collapsing severely recently. The County Government Construction Bureau convened representatives from all sectors on the 5th to hold a meeting to protect the embankment. The meeting decided (1) that all fields within 600 feet of the riverbank in Yao Ge Port would be subject to a small embankment protection donation area and a small amount of work to expand the embankment; (2) to raise funds to purchase four tons of stones to build the embankment; (3) in addition to raising funds locally, the Construction Bureau would send a letter to various shipping companies to subsidize 4,000 yuan; (4) that the embankment was in danger and could not wait. Borrow money from the Finance Bureau first and start work on the 10th.

Jiaxing

County Executive Committee selected. The term of office of the executive committee of the Jiaxing County Party Department has expired. Chen Naihe and other 22 people were selected at the Fourth County Congress and submitted for review and selection. Appointed commissioners to report on land and assist staff. The county assigned each member to go to various districts to provide assistance on the ground.

The Nanhuan Zhuang robbery case was solved. Wang Zuocai's family in Nanhuan Zhuang, Xupoqiao Township, Jiaxing, was robbed by bandits and injured. It is now learned that the bandits in this case have been arrested by the water police, including Zhu Jinde and Zhang A Jin and others, and the stolen goods and evidence have been recovered. The water police district sent them to the court for trial. It was learned from the trial that the landlady and neighbor of the victim, Blind Aunt San, was the mother-in-law of the bandit Zhu Jinde and had the suspicion of instigating the case. Therefore, the blind woman has been detained for investigation.

Hangzhou

Scheduled meeting for construction loans. The Finance and Construction Departments of Zhejiang Province need 2.4 million yuan for construction in the next four months, starting this month, but the construction bonds have not yet been issued. Therefore, they borrowed from the banking industry. However, the amount of the loan was too large and it was difficult to raise. They could only barely raise 600,000 to 700,000 yuan. Therefore, the Finance and Construction Departments decided to convene representatives from the chambers of commerce and the banking industry in the five counties of Hangzhou, Jiaxing, Huzhou, Ningbo, and Shaoxing in Hangzhou on the 10th to discuss the loan method. The construction bonds will still be used as collateral. It is also heard that because the original number of members of the Construction Bond Fund Management Committee was too small, it is planned to add three to five more members.

Solving the problem of the management of public funds and assets. The Department of Civil Affairs of Zhejiang Province submitted a proposal to the provincial government for decision. The original public fund and asset committees in various counties had many names and different organizations. They were all cancelled and new regulations were drafted by the department. After careful organization, the Department of Finance was immediately requested to send personnel to discuss and determine the principles. However, the detailed measures have not yet been decided. The Department of Finance sent a letter to the Department of Civil Affairs yesterday, requesting the department to take charge of drafting them. The second review meeting will be held on a scheduled date. It is said that this case will be resolved soon.

The opening of the Hangping Highway has been rescheduled. The Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bureau announced that the Hangping Road has been completed and was originally scheduled to open on the 23rd. Now it has been advanced and will be held on the 15th of this month.

Villagers petition to change the village boundaries. The former village of Yaosi, near Wanshi, was assigned to the joint village organized by Jiayi Zhang by the Huangba Village and Neighborhood Preparatory Committee. Recently, villagers Wang Laifa and others submitted a petition to the county government stating various reasons for their willingness to belong to Wanshi, because the villagers of Wanshi and Yaosi are of the same clan, have the same customs, and are located in a mountain area with frequent banditry. The Wanshi Security Corps has been in operation for many years and can protect the village. Therefore, the villagers do not want to belong to Jiayi Zhang and have petitioned the Village and Neighborhood Preparatory Committee of the county government.

Implementing the Party's Education Policy Proposal 62

▲ Original Proposal by Zhu Jiahua and Chu Minyi

At the Third Plenary Session, Zhu Jiahua and Chu Minyi jointly proposed a plan to vigorously implement the Party's education policy. After review by the education group, it was decided to submit it to the Political Council for discussion. The proposal is recorded as follows:

Education is the foundation of a nation and the mother of all revolutionary construction. Therefore, when the Party began its political tutelage, it established the purpose and implementation policy of education ("The Education Purpose and Its Implementation Policy Proposal Determined by the Brothers at the Third National Congress") so that it could be effectively implemented along this path. This would not only sweep away the bad consequences of past education, but also lay the foundation for the construction of the Three Principles of the People. However, in the past year, chaos has arisen one after another, and the revolutionary order and construction achieved through past efforts have almost been destroyed. The Party's original education policy has therefore been unable to advance. Now that the rebellion has been completely quelled and the obstacles have been removed, we must, in our deep reflection and sorrow, have the greatest determination and effort to realize the Party's education policy. Politics and education go hand in hand. The development of education depends on political stability, but if we want to promote the people's ability to self-govern and create a sound political order, nothing is more important than the popularization of education.

The Party's education policy has clear regulations for various education facilities. For the sake of the education of the entire country, we should take into consideration all aspects and avoid bias. However, considering the current national environment and the needs of the people, there must be a distinction between priorities and urgency. Now that political tutelage has just begun, the Party's greatest responsibility is to promote local autonomy and develop the national economy. To achieve this goal, we must do our best to eliminate illiteracy and increase production. Our country has never had accurate education statistics. According to recent surveys, the total population of the country is 444,715,4951 people, with approximately 42,560,000 out-of-school children and approximately 21,160,000 out-of-school adults. The total number of out-of-school people in the country is approximately 25,272,000. This survey has not been very accurate, so in reality, the number is likely to be even higher. Even based on this, the number of illiterate people in the country exceeds half of the population. It is clearly impossible for a people with the majority uneducated to exercise self-government and civil rights. Our country's economy is backward and production efficiency is declining. Taking grain as an example, according to the customs survey in the 16th year of the Republic of China, the total value of imported rice, wheat, and flour was as high as 135,605,000 taels. Our country has always been proud of its abundant agricultural production, but the result is such. It is truly lamentable. Therefore, if we want to save the bankruptcy of the national economy today, we must first strive to increase production efficiency. Based on these two major needs, we believe that the fundamental education that must be urgently implemented at present is compulsory national education, adult literacy education, and vocational education, all centered on cultivating national life skills.

However, to implement compulsory national education and adult literacy education, a large number of teachers must first be trained. At a standard of one teacher for every 250,000 people, more than 10 million teachers are needed to meet the demand. Such a huge need cannot be met without establishing many specialized schools. Moreover, these teachers have a special national mission and should receive special training that cannot be equated with ordinary education. Therefore, normal schools should be established independently and not be appendages of other schools. The length of schooling should be increased, training should be intensified, treatment should be improved, and the new salary of primary school teachers should be raised to create a sound foundation for normal school education. At the same time, incumbent primary school teachers and private school teachers should be trained separately during holidays each year. The lack of good primary school teachers has become a major problem. According to the statistics of the Zhejiang Education Department in the 17th year, only 41% of the province's primary school teachers had received normal school education, while the remaining 59% had not. The general private school teachers are not included. If these unqualified teachers are severely cracked down on, it is feared that the number of out-of-school people will increase even more during this transition period. Therefore, we have to actively plan and remedy the situation.

Vocational education has long been neglected in our country. The various vocational schools run by various provinces are mostly based on books, lack experimental equipment, and do not correspond to the local production environment. After graduation, there is no suitable outlet or guarantee. Therefore, the effect is equal to zero. In the future, we must vigorously correct the previous malpractices. The establishment of schools must be based on adapting to the local production needs as the main condition. Experimental factories should be set up in industrial areas and agricultural experiment stations should be set up in agricultural areas. On the one hand, they are used for students to practice, and on the other hand, they are the basis for transforming local production. We should also prepare for their livelihood and provide reliable guarantees so that they can achieve the goal of making the best use of their talents, land, materials, and flow. At the same time, vocational education should be implemented in the army for future reclamation, road construction, and other production purposes. This can not only turn profit into profit, but also be a fundamental plan to eliminate war, save the country, and save danger.

The Party's education policy takes equal educational opportunity as a basic principle. However, the current school education is clearly the privilege of a few wealthy people. The general poor children not only have no hope of receiving secondary education, but also cannot receive primary education. If this deformed education system is not fundamentally broken, the goal of universal education will never be achieved. Therefore, we advocate that all schools in the country should be free of charge so that poor youth can develop their talents. However, given the current financial difficulties, it is impossible to achieve this in a short time. We can only first exempt tuition fees for Party-run compulsory schools, adult literacy schools, and normal schools. The remaining secondary and above schools will first set up a certain number of free places and increase them year by year. When the education fees are sufficient, they will be fully exempted. The state should also subsidize and reward those who are interested in studying advanced academics. This is the minimum necessary condition for implementing the Party's education policy. Otherwise, even if we want to vigorously promote universal education, what can we do if the facts do not allow it? Finally, what we urgently need to fundamentally solve is the problem of education funding. If there is no sufficient preparation and guarantee for education funding, all plans will become pie in the sky. Judging from the current situation of education funding, it is not only insufficient to promote the Party's education policy, but it is also difficult to maintain the status quo. Therefore, for short-term solutions, we must first implement the already determined education funding. For long-term solutions, the central government and various provinces should stipulate 20% to 30% of the annual revenue as education funding, and an independent guarantee system must be established. We must also break the past fallacy of "local education is run with local funds." The central government should plan in a unified way to make education develop evenly in various places. Only in this way can the Party's education policy be thoroughly implemented. (To be continued)

The Jiangsu Middle School Association Requests a Meeting 63

Jiangsu Education Funding Committee

Wang Maozu, Xue Deyi, and Zhou Hougui, standing committee members of the Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Association, submitted a document to Niu, Director of the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office, stating that the annual funding for provincial middle schools cannot be maintained according to the budget. It is hoped that the director will review the matter and quickly convene a meeting of the funding committee to discuss relief measures to facilitate progress. It is noted that the schools' operations have been increasing year by year, but the budget is still based on old standards. When the previous funding committee discussed the budget for this year, it included middle school tuition and dormitory fees and school agricultural income into the budget. The representatives of the association present at the meeting stated the reasons, but could not arouse the sympathy of the committee members present. Therefore, this year's budget has actually decreased by about 20% compared to the previous year. Previously, the schools' funding shortages could be compensated by tuition and dormitory fees. Now, there is no room for flexibility. If the budget for this year is prepared in accordance with the budget issued by the Education Department, the original operations will inevitably be suspended if the revenue and expenditure are to be balanced, let alone expanded. Therefore, the budget prepared by each school has to exceed the budget. Up to now, the budget has not been prepared. Now, fortunately, you have returned to the province to preside over the matter. Therefore, we sincerely appeal to you to convene a meeting of the funding committee to find a fundamental solution. In addition, how should the temporary budget for the 18th year be allocated? It should also be announced immediately. How should the boarding expenses of normal school students be compensated in this autumn when rice is like pearls and firewood is like cinnamon? When should the security deposits of this year's normal school graduates be returned for sightseeing? These matters cannot be resolved without the funding committee. We beg you to understand our difficulties and approve the convening of a meeting of the funding committee to discuss relief measures to facilitate the progress of education.

This City

The Municipal Education Bureau Restricts the Admission of Transfer Students at All Levels 64

Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau: The number of transfer students in schools at all levels in the city has been increasing recently, and the level of students varies, which has made education difficult. The reasons for the transfer are as follows: 1. Changes in the occupation of parents and brothers, and the relocation of families, often cause students to change schools. 2. A large number of students request transfers because their level is too low to be promoted to the next grade. 3. Bad conduct and repeated admonitions have not been corrected, and the school authorities have to order them to withdraw from school. 4. There are many who are ambitious and want to leapfrog grades. 5. Some are dissatisfied with the school's measures and voluntarily request a transfer. 6. The school is closed (referring to a private school). Except for the first and sixth reasons, which are unavoidable and should be accommodated, other transfer students are either too low in level, or have bad conduct, or are ambitious and arrogant, or are nitpicking and arbitrarily attacking. If they are allowed to leave this school for another without restriction, it will not only cause problems in education, but also affect moral education. The future of education is very important. Therefore, the following measures are proposed to restrict the admission of transfer students in schools at all levels in the city: 1. Transfer students who have not studied in this school for more than one year shall not be given a graduation certificate. Primary school students under the age of 15 who have moved their home or have other legitimate reasons, and whose level is equal, and who have a transfer certificate and a letter of introduction from the principal, are not subject to this restriction. 2. Transfer students must first present their transfer certificate or score sheet for verification before being allowed to take the entrance examination. 3. Schools shall not accept requests for student transfers after classes have been going on for more than two weeks. 4. Those who are of poor level and bad conduct, and who are deemed by the school authorities to be hopeless and ordered to withdraw from school, shall not be allowed to transfer. 5. Students from afar who have not yet prepared their transfer certificate and are deemed satisfactory after the entrance examination may be allowed to temporarily audit.

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's Business Report at the Sixth Municipal Congress (5) 68

(3) Upcoming Business

1. Increase the number of classes in municipal schools. Compulsory education in this city has not yet been popularized. The number of classes in each municipal school should be increased to avoid leaving out students who have registered. At the beginning of each semester, the bureau will select the municipal school with the most registered students and add classes as appropriate. However, it is still not possible to accommodate all of them, and more will need to be added one after another. We will try our best to increase the number of classes within the limits of economic possibility to reduce the number of out-of-school children.

2. Repair municipal school buildings. It is not possible to repair the school buildings of each municipal school at the same time without this financial resources. We have to prioritize the projects. The Municipal School Building Repair Committee has made overall plans, sorted out the construction fees collected by various municipal schools, surveyed the projects, determined the order of repairs, and prepared a budget, which the bureau will submit to the municipal government for approval.

(4) Difficulties

1. Failure to unify educational rights

(1) Educational rights in the concessions. This special municipality is divided into concessions, and the powers are not unified, which makes it difficult to handle matters. Private schools with a general purpose other than education rely on the concessions and harm young people. The bureau has taken measures to ban them, but some have disobeyed in public and obeyed in private, while others have moved to avoid them. Therefore, there is no education to speak of in the concessions. It is not easy to thoroughly rectify the situation without taking back the educational rights of the concessions.

(2) Provincial educational rights. This special municipality does not belong to the scope of the province, but is an administrative region directly under the National Government. However, there are provincial schools in the urban area, and the educational assets that this city should receive have not yet been fully transferred. This is also a lack of unified powers, which hinders the progress of business.

2. The exhaustion of educational funds

This city has a dense population and prosperous industry and commerce. School education and social education need to be actively promoted. As there are many projects, the funds have also increased. Although the educational funds of this city have been repeatedly increased in recent years, they are still difficult to allocate due to the amount of work that needs to be done. Therefore, the budget has been reduced again and again, which is like cutting one's feet to fit one's shoes. The lack of economic resources is indeed a difficulty in developing education.

(5) Hopes

1. Hope that the Party Headquarters and citizens will cooperate

Education is related to the foundation of the country. The bureau's responsibility is to do its best to develop education. We also hope that the Party Headquarters will lead the citizens and the municipal government to cooperate to make the city's education more developed.

2. Hope for unified educational rights

The lack of unified powers and the division of policies hinder the progress of education. The city's educational administration feels quite constrained, and all facilities have not been thoroughly implemented. We deeply hope that the educational rights in this city will be unified as soon as possible to facilitate the function of educational administration (End)
