Free Talk

A Laughing Matter 77

—Hai Ke

A: Why did you cancel your engagement with your fiancée?

B: Because every time I went to her house, I always heard her parrot calling out, "Old Bing, kiss the young lady!"

A: That couldn't be better.

B: But I'm not Old Bing!

A: After you got married, did you feel any differences from when you were engaged?

B: How could there not be? When we were engaged, my wife was satisfied just sitting on my lap. Now she's really sitting on top of me!

A: Do you know the difference between a fake linen handkerchief and a real linen handkerchief?

B: It's easy to tell.

A: How?

B: My real linen handkerchief is often stolen, but the fake linen handkerchief has never been lost.

Mrs. A: Your husband has traveled far across the ocean this time. He must be on the Pacific Ocean right now. Are you thinking about him every moment?

Mrs. B: I'm very relieved because he's always been used to swimming in the Hongkou swimming pool.

Records of Talking About Beasts Around the Stove 78

— Zheng Yimei

The spring cold is still sharp. I stayed at home and didn't go out. Suddenly, Xu Zihanqing arrived with a light and swift step, bringing the joy of a rare visitor to a secluded valley. Hanqing is a zoologist. My friends and I pestered him to talk about beasts to break the silence. Thus, I recorded some of what we discussed on the left.

Zebras are produced in the southeastern part of both North and South America. However, their reproduction is not prolific, and they are difficult to tame. They cannot be used to serve people like ordinary horses. Their color is white or light yellow, encircled by black or brown stripes, resembling a rabbit. It is quite a spectacle. English and German zoologists, lamenting that Europe does not produce these horses, devised a method to obtain them. Their method is quite interesting. They cause black horses and white horses to mate. During mating, they specifically emit a strange electric light. Sometimes it turns brown, sometimes black, sometimes yellow, and sometimes white. They make these colors flash alternately in the horses' eyes. When they conceive and give birth, the patterns are exactly like a zebra's. This is also quite extraordinary.

Sichuan has many mountains. Monkeys dwell in the caves and crevices, forming groups of hundreds or thousands. Therefore, Li Bai has the line, "The monkeys' cries on both banks cannot be stopped, my light boat has already passed ten thousand mountains." Monkeys love to eat fruit. Those who capture them often lure them with fruit. They load the boat full of fruit and anchor at the edge of the stream at night. The people hide in the belly of the boat, completely silent. When the monkeys see the fruit piled up, they all climb over rocks and trees to reach it, swallowing peaches and gnawing plums, enjoying themselves immensely. The boat is deliberately equipped with a mechanism. When pressed, the deck tilts. The monkeys stealing fruit all fall into the boat. Monkeys fear being killed and also hate seeing blood. Therefore, they deliberately kill a chicken and drain its blood. This frightens them so much that they dare not move, and they are all tied up with ropes. There is a saying, "Kill a chicken to show the monkey." This saying has its origins.

New Sparrow Talk 79

— A Guest Returning with Refreshed Eyes

Among today's entertainment devices that can anesthetize the whole country and gradually spread to the Atlantic Ocean, none is like mahjong. My friend Gu Zinan told me about two recent small news stories related to mahjong within the last ten days. Therefore, I compiled them into the "New Sparrow Talk" as follows.

There is a good match in this. A man named Chen Yongquan was asked to celebrate someone's birthday last Tuesday. He was strongly pulled into joining a mahjong game by the guests. Yongquan is usually timid in such situations, mainly due to economic pressure. On that day, they played twelve rounds. His losses were less than one silver dollar. However, he was already sweating as if steamed, and his face was the color of pig liver. Yesterday, Zinan heard someone say that Yongquan had already found a beautiful wife and would be getting married on the upcoming Sunday (March 16th). Zinan further investigated the matter. Only then did he learn that the good match was found in the mahjong game. On that day, the mahjong game was at its peak. The player above Yongquan was the dealer, discarding a four of characters to eat a seven of characters. The player below, a young lady, had thrown away a red dragon as her first discard. Yongquan then changed one red dragon into three. As the situation became tense, he even discarded one red dragon, waiting for a five or eight of characters. He drew one himself and won. The young lady was waiting for a closed six of characters. Everyone blamed Yongquan for not discarding the red dragon earlier. The young lady smiled and said, "What are you saying? The dealer was obviously going for a pure suit. Sacrificing the red dragon to avoid giving a big win is truly stable and skillful." An old man standing behind the young lady nodded in agreement. During the dinner, he asked Yongquan about his family finances and living situation in detail. It turned out that the old man was the young lady's father. He knew his daughter's heart had been won, so he seized the opportunity to create a good match. The next day, he hired a matchmaker. In less than three days, they had agreed on the marriage. Discarding one red dragon led to a good thing. How wonderful! Therefore, it is said, "There is a good match in this."

Gaining Ten Thousand and Losing One Thousand Zinan also said, "Things have their fortunes and misfortunes. They cannot be reasoned with normal logic." The day after Yongquan's mahjong game, I visited a friend in Ximen for some business. My friend was in a mahjong game, so I stood aside and joined the crowd watching the game. One player was waiting for a three, six, or nine of bamboos. He suddenly kept the one of characters he drew, discarding the nine of bamboos, abandoning the three wait for a one wait. After shuffling the tiles twice, he drew one himself and won. Some laughed at him for not knowing the rules of the game. Others envied his lucky hand. The person behind the player across from him said, "Amazing skill! How could he have foreseen it?" It turned out that the opponent had a pair of white dragons and had discarded a red dragon. He had been waiting for a one or four of characters for a long time and had suffered this setback. That person was also very pleased with himself, tirelessly recounting when he knew that his opponent was close to winning and when he knew that he was waiting for characters. I didn't want to wait any longer and left. Now I hear that the opponent is very resentful. The two sides had originally planned to jointly invest in a business, with an investment of one thousand yuan. Now he has made excuses to cancel the contract, as there was no contract signed, so he is not bound by breach of contract. Isn't this gaining ten thousand and losing one thousand? I didn't have time to ask for that person's name. Zinan also didn't mention it. How unlucky that person is! Chen Yongquan is truly lucky.

A Rare Story of Discovering Bird Shapes in a Tree 80

— Xiaochang

The other day, I attended a celebratory banquet at my classmate Cheng Jun's house. During the meal, I heard Cheng Jun's uncle, Wang Baotian, tell a story about discovering bird shapes in a tree. It was truly a rare story. Therefore, I transcribed it here for the research of scholars across the country.

Wang is over sixty years old. He is from the northern village of Lin'an. His family's business is selling trees. Thirty years ago, Wang went to Yuqian to sell trees. He bought a chestnut tree for two hundred silver coins. In the middle of the tree, there was a tree growing in the mountain valley, about thirty feet long and three feet one or two inches in circumference. It was called the "Bird Stop," because the branches and leaves of the tree were covered with thorns, so birds could not stop on it. Wang had heard his ancestors say that if the circumference of a "Bird Stop" tree was two feet, there would be bird shapes inside the tree. However, very large trees of this type are extremely rare, because their texture is unusually dense and they do not grow easily. Any tree with a circumference of about one foot must be over a hundred years old. Therefore, after Wang obtained the tree, he removed its branches and split it in two to see what was inside. Unexpectedly, there were dozens of bird shapes in the tree, each with a different posture, scattered within a ten-foot section of the tree's middle. Wang was overjoyed and carried the split tree back home, intending to split it further into several thin planks. However, the bird shapes that had already been split were very blurred and incomplete. Wang's colleague, an old man, learned about this. He told Wang, "When splitting a tree with a saw, if you saw it for too long, the saw will get hot. When splitting a tree that has bird shapes, you must avoid the saw getting hot. Because once the saw gets hot, the bird shapes in the tree will definitely become blurred. If you want to avoid this problem, you should prepare several saws when splitting. After sawing for a short time, switch to another saw. If you rotate the saws in this way, the saw will not get hot." Wang followed his advice and split the tree again. The bird shapes were indeed very clear. This was truly a rare treasure. After removing the outer edges of the tree, a total of twenty-five planks were split, each with bird shapes on both sides. Wang sold them one by one (they were used to make screens and tabletops, which were quite valuable, selling for fifty or sixty silver dollars per plank. Four of them were bought by a newly appointed magistrate to present to his superiors. These were worth a total of four hundred and ten silver dollars). This tree earned a total of over one thousand five hundred silver dollars. Wang's family was originally poor. After receiving this benefit, they gradually became well-off. Now they have some assets and can live comfortably.

The Wedding Night 81

— Jingbai

With the eastward spread of Western customs, the voices of free love and free marriage often resound in our ears. Young men and women all regard them as golden rules. As for the old-fashioned marriage system, the parents' orders and the matchmaker's words, if you talk to today's youth about them, they will all cover their ears and run away, scoffing at them. Unexpectedly, my old friend Yuan, as an extremely modern person, recently had an old-fashioned marriage. The result was sweet and fulfilling, leading him to make extremely brilliant remarks. Yuan's words were so wonderful, how could I not record them?

My old friend Yuan is studying at a certain middle school. He is intelligent and studious, and his grades are the best among his peers. Recently, he held a beautiful wedding ceremony. The next day, dozens of classmates went to congratulate him. I was also fortunate enough to attend and enjoy the lavish feast. The group strongly urged the newlywed to announce the wedding process and the secrets of the first night. Yuan looked around. There was no one else in the room but his fellow students. Joking and teasing were common among them. Therefore, he had no need to be shy. He announced it to them frankly. Everyone listened intently, more focused than when they were receiving lessons in the classroom. Yuan ordered the cups to be washed and more wine to be poured in preparation for both recording his words and drinking. The Book of Han can be enjoyed with wine, and brilliant words can indeed add to the meal. Then, Yuan, with a smile on his face, made his brilliant remarks: "People say that old-fashioned marriages are blind marriages. I think that's a big mistake. Free love, when it comes to marriage, is the announcement of the end of love. There is no more progress to be made, and it becomes boring. Those who encounter misfortune are countless. Only old-fashioned marriages are the starting point of love. The romance in the boudoir will only increase. As for the wedding process, since it was old-fashioned, there is no so-called process. But the joy of the first night will never be forgotten. When the night is quiet, I entered the bridal chamber. There was a beautiful woman, sitting silently in beautiful makeup. Looking up, I saw the bright moon in the sky, and three stars entered the room. I suspected that the Guanghan Palace was not necessarily in the clouds. So, I slowly approached her seat and slowly started a conversation. She was shy and seemed overwhelmed with emotion. Then, we held hands and entered the bedchamber. The situation inside can only be shared with those who have experienced it and cannot be told to outsiders. On the other hand, with free marriages, the path is well-worn. Can there be such mystery and joy? Most of my colleagues have not experienced this. Whether his words are true or not, I record it here as a reference for the future."

Bits of Common Knowledge 82

— Tang Bihua

The newspaper vendors who follow rickshaws at the wharf station are the most unreliable. You often easily buy stale newspapers from the previous day.

Do not be fooled by those on the street impersonating demobilized soldiers and peddling jewels. Also, do not be greedy for cheap ivory chopsticks or soap. Otherwise, you will lose more than you gain.

When traveling, if you have luggage, be sure to copy the number on the luggage tag into your diary. If you lose your luggage tag, you can report it to the station at your destination, explaining the number, the number of pieces of luggage, and the items inside. You can have your belongings returned to you without fail.

Do not take pictures with friends you meet by chance. If you encounter a bad person, trouble will arise as a result, damaging your reputation. You must be careful.

Detailed Record of the Abolition of Prostitution Lottery in Hangzhou 83

— Songlu, reporting from Hangzhou

The Hangzhou Municipal Government, in order to completely relieve the suffering of prostitutes, has initiated a phased lottery system to abolish prostitution. March 1st was the date for the first implementation of the lottery. Because I considered this event unprecedented in Hangzhou, I felt I must go and observe it. However, I was accustomed to waking up late, so I was afraid that I would lose sleep at the critical moment. Therefore, the day before, I hired a car with a friend to go to Gongchen Bridge and stayed at Dafang Inn so that I could go and observe it at ease the next day.

The homes announce the news at dawn The next day at dawn, I was awakened by the sound of knocking on doors in the neighboring houses. Upon asking, I learned that it was the police announcing the news to each house by calling out to the drum girls. So we quickly got up and brushed our teeth.

The venue at Wang Zhuang is solemn and orderly The lottery venue for the day was set up at the Ronghua Theater. There were not many seats. Yu Jimin, the section chief of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the matter, had arrived before me. When he saw me, he led me to the reporters' seat and told me about the preparations for the lottery. At this time, the venue was quite solemn and orderly. Dozens of prostitutes had arrived and were seated in the front row. Their madams and aunties were seated in the boxes upstairs. There was a couplet hanging in front of the stage, which read: "(Alas, the leaves and flowers compete for beauty. They flutter and fly, defiling the northern villages of the Sui Dynasty. May the orioles and swallows strive to be the first to welcome the east wind to gather in the imperial gardens.)" Although the sentences were not well-crafted, they were still interesting. To the left of the stage, behind the seats for photographs, there was a display of red flowers, which were prepared as identifiers for the abolished prostitutes to wear. There were eight characters written on a red silk banner: "(Escape the fire pit, restore your personality.)" This was also quite alert.

Alert and interesting slogans Slogans were posted all around the venue. The sentences were mostly alert and interesting, such as "(Prostitutes who are drawn to be abolished have accumulated the virtue of their ancestors.)" "(Once you are drawn to be abolished, you are still a pure girl.)" "(From now on, you will see the light of day.)" "(It is too late to awaken when you are old and faded.)" etc.

Mac's speech makes the hall laugh After the opening remarks, Chairman Li Zicai finished his speech, and representatives from various agencies spoke in succession. Then, Mike, a police advisor from the Department of Civil Affairs, gave a speech. Mike was not accustomed to speaking Chinese and spoke in English. As soon as he finished speaking, he made the whole hall laugh.

The number of people who should be abolished this time The number of prostitutes who should be abolished this time was as follows: There were originally thirty-eight first-class prostitutes in Gongchen Bridge. Excluding three who had stopped working and twelve who were supported by patrons, one-sixth of the twenty-three should be drawn, totaling four. There were two hundred and ninety-seven second-class prostitutes. Excluding one hundred and twenty-eight who were supported by patrons, one-sixth of the one hundred and sixty-nine should be drawn, totaling twenty-eight. The total was thirty-one.

The lottery procedure is precise The lottery tickets were made of bamboo, with the words "abolished" and "retained" written on them. They were each wrapped in white paper. When drawing the tickets, the seal had to be broken and examined. Each prostitute drew her own ticket. The method was truly meticulous and strict.

Various interesting anecdotes during the lottery There were many interesting anecdotes during the lottery. Here are a few excerpts: (1) First-class prostitute Chuchu did not arrive that day due to smallpox. After proof was provided, her madam was allowed to draw on her behalf. Unexpectedly, she drew "abolished." So this old madam, who was over sixty years old, temporarily took the prostitute's place. (2) Second-class prostitute Lin Zhicao was over fifty years old. She still sang and entertained people on weekdays. She also drew the word "abolished" that day. The audience laughed when she wore a red flower on her chest. (3) Second-class prostitute Hongdi was twenty-eight years old. She was a clerk supported by patrons at Zhu Zhang's place. She arrived that day wearing a long skirt and short coat. She was calm and composed. When she was summoned, she said to the person checking her photos, "I have already paid off my debt and am willing to be a good woman. Now, please return my certificate so that I can go home with my guest (her lover)."

Why shed tears after being drawn? On that day, the prostitutes who were drawn to be abolished all shed tears and cried bitterly. Some even lay on the ground and cried uncontrollably. Alas, was this because they were surrounded by the environment, or was it their nature? I truly do not understand.

The cries at Jiliang Hall shake the earth Afterwards, I went to visit Jiliang Hall. When I arrived, the cries shook the earth, making it unbearable to hear. Some who recognized me pulled at my clothes and begged for help. I smiled and said, "You are jumping out of the fire pit. You should be happy, why are you so sad? Soon, your patrons will come to marry you and take you home for a reunion." The prostitutes were still skeptical. Then, the representatives of the Women's Association, Lin Song and Wang Wei, spoke in succession, earnestly advising them. Only then did they stop crying, express their gratitude, and smile through their tears.

Various after-the-fact tidbits of news After the reporters left Jiliang Hall, they went to sit in a teahouse. The street talk and gossip were varied. Here are a few: (1) First-class prostitute Chuchu originally used her own daughter as a prostitute. Now she has been drawn to be abolished and has a debt of four thousand yuan. (2) Second-class prostitute Liu Xiuying, although she worked independently, spent lavishly on weekdays. Her debt also reached more than nine hundred yuan. (3) Wenjun was a leader among the second-class prostitutes. She had elderly parents and a young child still in swaddling clothes. They all relied on her for a living. Once she was drawn, her elderly parents were extremely sad and heartbroken. (4) Second-class prostitute Miaoyun had a thriving business and was good at saving money. She had already saved more than five hundred silver coins. She was reluctant to leave this fire pit. Being drawn this time can be said to be self-inflicted trouble.

A Strange Drama After the Abolition of Prostitution in Hangzhou 84

— Songlu, reporting from Hangzhou

The Hangzhou Municipal Government, in order to improve women's rights and liberate women, has initiated a lottery system to abolish prostitution. The circumstances of its progress have already been reported in yesterday's draft. Unexpectedly, a strange change has occurred that is beyond expectations. The prostitutes who were abolished and kept in Jiliang Hall were completely robbed by madams and others. The matter is truly shocking to hear. I have explored and described its process and sent it by express mail to the Free Talk section.

Previously, the Public Security Bureau kept the follow-up measures for the abolition of prostitution strictly secret. Therefore, the prostitutes who were abolished at that time all cried with tears, as if the pain in Jiliang Hall was worse than in prison. After the lottery, these forty-odd abolished prostitutes were sent to Jiliang Hall together. The rooms in the hall were quite cramped. At this time, there was a sense of few rooms and many people, making it difficult to find space to sit. At the same time, the pimps and madams of the brothels were seeking help everywhere, asking to be temporarily released on bail. Dai Shuming, the chief of the third district, considered it reasonable and granted their request. At one time, more than twenty people were released on bail. When Yu Jimin, the second section chief of the Public Security Bureau, heard about this, he strongly disapproved, saying that since the prostitutes had been abolished, how could they be temporarily released on bail? He ordered them to be recalled one by one and sent to the hall. When the general pimps and madams heard this news, they felt that the government was going back on its word and were quite indignant. At the same time, rumors spread, saying that these abolished prostitutes would be sent into the city. So they gathered local hooligans and thugs and carried out a robbery at Jiliang Hall. Sure enough, Jiliang Hall was completely unprepared and was broken into. All the prostitutes were robbed. Afterwards, the district authorities sent police to pursue and arrest them, but they gained nothing. They ordered the pimps and madams of the brothels to hand over the people. The brothels claimed that the incident occurred at Jiliang Hall and that it was difficult to be responsible for tracking them down. As of the time of this submission, there was still no proper solution. However, Gongchen Bridge is a small place with inconvenient transportation, and prostitutes are easily identified. It will not be difficult to catch them one by one.

Each bank adopts a self-preservation policy.

The circulation of discount notes is temporarily suspended.

Large shortages create a tense situation.

The aftermath of the Yuda Bank's troubles

In the past two days, due to the Yuda Bank's suspension, the money houses adopted a self-preservation policy, and the circulation of discount notes was suddenly suspended, creating a tense situation. The rumors were rampant and unstoppable, so trading in the market turned cold. Bank receipts were huge, totaling over 10 million in notes, exchange, goods, and pledges. Special receipts totaled over 10 million (including transfers to money houses). The amount of goods entering the warehouse was truly shocking, said to be over 10 million. The money houses did not have this huge amount of cash on hand, and turnover was particularly tight. Oil Market: Asphalt Arrivals Are Scarce, Seeing Price Increases 99

Last year, due to the late arrival of asphalt from the Jingyi area of Hubei, Shanghai merchants relied on the Zhejiang route. The mountain asphalt in Jinhua and Lanxi, Zhejiang, was not as abundant as in previous years. Moreover, the asphalt from Jiaxing, which is closest to Shanghai, was even more scarce. This led to the market showing new products and immediately rising in price. Shanghai merchants were fortunate to have the supply from Taizhou and Jiangxi, which barely sustained the supply during the three winter months. Since the beginning of spring, there has been no attention paid to the Zhejiang route, because Ezhou's annual output was abundant. There were no large shipments before the end of the year, but there were concerns about a flood of arrivals after the Lunar New Year. The shipments from Hankou arrived intermittently, but the foreign firms had already purchased them during the end of the year, so the arrivals were still insufficient. As a result, the Macheng Hong Pan immediately showed strength, opening at 12.8 taels and quickly rising to 13 taels, and recently to 13.2 taels. The famous Jing was at 13.4 taels, the Zhijiang Zhong Zhu also at 13.2 taels, the Ping Jing at 13 taels, and the Jinshi at 12.8 taels, all at the same price, already better than the Hong Pan by 4 qian. Moreover, due to the lack of supply, there were no stockpiles. Shanghai merchants had to wait for the goods to arrive, so the current oil in Shanghai was quite scarce, and the selling price was slightly higher.

Cuban Embassy Relocates South 100

The Chargé d'Affaires Arrives in Shanghai with Case Files Yesterday Morning

Cuban Chargé d'Affaires, Mr. and Mrs. Calixto, arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin on the Tongzhou vessel. They were originally scheduled to arrive on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, but due to bad weather and hurricanes at sea, they were delayed until 7:30 AM yesterday. Cuban Minister General Piedra had personally gone to the dock to welcome them the day before yesterday, waiting until 7:00 PM, but the ship had not yet arrived, so he returned to his residence. Yesterday morning, the Cuban Minister specially sent the Chinese secretary, Mr. Hu Zhenting, to the dock to take care of the matter. The External Affairs Office also sent Mr. Tang Shixuan to welcome them. After disembarking, the Chargé d'Affaires took a car to the Triumph Hotel to rest. All the case files and documents of the Cuban Embassy were temporarily stored there. According to the Chargé d'Affaires, the embassy building should be found and moved into by mid-January, and official business will begin then.

Resolutions of the Municipal Representative Assembly on Party, Government, and Police Reports 101

Resolution on the Party Affairs Report: Since the fifth session of the Executive and Supervisory Committee took office, the municipal party affairs have made significant progress in the past year in terms of party organization, propaganda, training, and spirit and form. Although various plans could not be fully implemented due to the constraints of the situation, the result of a year's efforts and struggles is that the party's organization has gradually become complete and solid from being scattered, and the party's command has gradually become unified from being divergent. Therefore, it can instruct each other and respond appropriately, clearing up the chaotic situation of the past and laying a solid foundation for the future. The General Assembly is satisfied with this. In the past year, in order to eliminate feudal forces and consolidate the revolutionary regime, the party vigorously advocated troop reduction and implemented demobilization plans, causing reactionary warlords to rebel one after another because they could not fulfill their desire for separatist self-interest. Zhang, Gui, Feng, and Tang rose one after another, the people's hearts were shaken, and the country was in turmoil. At this time, Shanghai was an important rear area, and all reactionary elements and remnants of feudalism wanted to rekindle their ashes and take the opportunity to make trouble. Crises were everywhere, and dangers were rampant. A little carelessness would lead to falling into the whirlpool of reaction. This can be seen from the changes in party headquarters in various places and the defection of comrades. However, our Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters, in this situation of overflowing torrents, can not only stand firm in the rapids without shaking, but also unify its will, concentrate its strength, and engage in continuous combat with reactionary forces, destroying the enemies' rising flames and relieving the central government's worries. The decisions were made in an instant, and the success or failure was determined by one move. Without the fifth session of the Executive and Supervisory Committee comrades, who were deeply rooted, loyal, and well-led, how could we have achieved this? This is not only adding a valuable record to the history of the municipal party, but also the deep appreciation of the delegates. Although the municipal party's measures in the past year have made considerable progress, there are still shortcomings everywhere. To summarize the main points, there are only two aspects: first, the work policy cannot be completely determined; second, the work methods cannot be improved in accordance with the times. In terms of the first point, most of the past work was to deal with the immediate situation. Treating the symptoms in a hurry and adapting to the times has been the supreme means, but there has been no overall decision on the party's work policy and work objects. As a result, although the hearts and minds of thousands of people have been inspired in the past year, they have worked hard day and night, exhausting their energy in paperwork and running around. However, the effect has little impact on the future of revolution and construction, and even less on people's livelihood and society. For this reason, social organizations are still feudal organizations, and social systems are still feudal systems. On top of this kind of feudal organization and system, to seek the realization of the party's doctrine is tantamount to planting seedlings on rocky fields and hoping for a harvest. Everyone knows that it is impossible. In terms of the second point, the work methods of party departments at all levels in the city mostly only have the outline of form, and there is very little practical effectiveness. Following the old ways and sticking to the rules, if this continues unchanged, it will decline again and again, and will fall into a state of paralysis and stagnation and will not be able to recover. Without knowing that the times have moved forward and the real environment is different due to the times and places, the work methods should be improved in order to adapt, let alone say anything else. In summary, the General Assembly, in addition to complying with all the laws and resolutions of the central government, makes the following instructions on the improvement of work policies and work methods for the work of party departments at all levels in the future: A. Work policies: (1) In the future, the power of the organization, propaganda, and training departments should be concentrated on the reform of the social system, so that the new social foundation of democracy can be gradually established. Feudal forces arise from within social organizations, and social organizations are based on social systems. Therefore, to eliminate social feudal forces, efforts should be concentrated on the reform of the social system. The core of the social system is nothing more than economics, politics, and morality. Although the reform of this economic, political, and moral social system is a matter of legislation and administration, the party headquarters should always fulfill its responsibilities of revolution, supervision, guidance, and correction. Moreover, Shanghai is the center of culture, and every move is enough to affect the whole country. In the past, the party has made efforts in the political movement to abolish the lunar calendar, the moral movement to abolish prostitution, and the economic cooperative movement. However, the whole of the social system is very broad, and it is impossible to shake the foundation of the old system that has been gradually accumulated for three thousand years with only the efforts of this scale. As for the implementation plan, it still needs to be reviewed and finalized by those who come later based on this principle. (2) In the future, we should do our best to promote and expand the anti-imperialist movement and seek the final success of the revolution. The party has made considerable achievements in eliminating domestic warlords in the past, but has not made significant achievements in the anti-imperialist movement. Shanghai is the base camp of international imperialism. All the encroachment of concessions and legal rights, and the economic and political aggression are also concentrated in Shanghai. Not only do we personally witness it and feel extremely painful, but also the inability to develop industry and commerce and the day-to-day decline are also most influenced by the economic oppression of imperialism. Therefore, in the future, we should strengthen our strength, expand our scope, and engage in continuous hand-to-hand combat. (3) In terms of the people, we should devote our efforts to the training of the four rights and the promotion of local self-government, so as to cultivate the people's knowledge and ability to participate in politics and establish a practical foundation for political tutelage. The era has been flying towards the stage of political tutelage and is advancing rapidly. The training of the people's political knowledge and ability is in urgent need. The party's work should quickly adapt to the requirements of this environment without the need for further discussion. Therefore, in the future, we should make multi-faceted efforts in party member training, mass training, and propaganda movements, so that Shanghai will be the advocate for the whole country and promote the early completion of the political tutelage work. B. Work methods: Regarding the party's internal work, although all past plans were very detailed, in fact, they often failed to implement the proposals and achieve corresponding results. The General Assembly heard the reports of the various departments and extracted the main points to make the following instructions: Regarding organizational work, in the Municipal Party Headquarters, each department acts on its own and does not communicate with each other. The progress of all work is due to the vertical lines being too strict, so the horizontal relationship cannot be connected. The differences between each other are multiplied, and the economic inefficiency of time, manpower, and financial resources is the worst. In the district party headquarters, the executive and supervisory committee members mostly hold concurrent positions outside and cannot assume their responsibilities. Most of the work is entrusted to the staff, and the staff cannot be autonomous in everything, so they delay and delay, resulting in a desolate and desolate image of the district party headquarters organization. In addition, the allocation of funds is not completely in accordance with the central government's standards, so the activity funds are often insufficient to meet the urgent needs of the work. In the district branch, due to occupational reasons, they cannot devote themselves to the progress of the work. All the branches are empty for a long time, and it is difficult to deliver letters, let alone other things. The party member congresses mostly fail to reach a quorum, and the meeting is lackluster and ends hastily, which has become a common phenomenon. Therefore, in the future, attention should be paid to the following points and earnestly corrected: (1) The work of the various departments of the municipal and district party headquarters should be made to echo each other and closely connect, so as to make their relationship increasingly close and achieve the effect of different paths leading to the same goal. (2) Within the possible scope, try to increase the funds of the district party headquarters, allocate living expenses and activity funds in a similar way, and strictly restrict the concurrent positions of its members outside. (3) The division of the location of the district branch, the allocation of the number of party members, and the distribution of the duties of the executive committee of the district branch should be closely noted. In the future, the work should be frequently supervised. Regarding propaganda work: First, the propaganda plan, in addition to the revolutionary commemorative festivals and all ordinary work, has not yet been effectively and persistently implemented on the points that should be publicized during the political tutelage period. Second, the propaganda methods mostly follow the old examples of gathering the upper-class people in society and giving public speeches, but they cannot use the inherent centralized opportunities of mass organizations to conduct planned propaganda. Third, the research on propaganda skills and the cultivation of propaganda talents cannot be closely linked with the two departments of organization and training, so that greater achievements cannot be made. Therefore, in the future, attention should be paid to the following points for correction: (1) In addition to vigorously implementing the above-mentioned three principles, the propaganda plan should focus on the seven movements issued by the central government, such as literacy, hygiene, cooperation, and domestic goods, which are most suitable for the time and space needs of Shanghai, and should be implemented effectively and in a planned way according to their urgency and importance. (2) The research on propaganda skills and the cultivation of talents should be mutually connected with the two departments of organization and training to make multi-faceted efforts. (3) In the future, the propaganda methods should use the inherent centralized opportunities of mass organizations to assign specialists to give regular and long-term speeches. Regarding training work, the party member training in the past was only limited to the enlightenment of party doctrine theory, and the theory and practice were not mutually connected. Moreover, the cultivation of party members' personality and morality was not fully paid attention to. In terms of party doctrine education, it was only limited to the school level, and there was no corresponding guidance for all cultural institutions and academic groups. Therefore, in the future, attention should be paid to the correction of the following points: (1) Party member training should be integrated into practical work and be the cultivation of organizational talents, propaganda talents, and training talents. (2) In addition to party doctrine training, party members should also be given party ethics and party ideology education. (3) In addition to schools and boy scouts, party doctrine education should also pay attention to the investigation and guidance of cultural institutions and academic groups. Regarding civil training work, in the past, it only involved the consolidation of groups and the handling of disputes, and very few achievements were made in the actual work of civil training. Therefore, the theory and essence of civil training have not been generally understood by the public, and even the staff has not had an appropriate concept, resulting in more disputes and more difficult consolidation. In the future, we should earnestly pay attention to the correction of the following points: (1) The policy of civil training should be based on the laws and resolutions issued by the central government and consider the methods of implementation. (2) All labor-capital conflicts should be resolved on the premise of "safeguarding the common survival of the people and the interests of the whole society." (3) The training staff should correct the concept of work so that the people and the party can establish a relationship, and should not isolate them with individuals. (4) Vigorously implement the work policy in the preceding paragraph and use the inherent centralized opportunities of mass organizations to devote all efforts to the seven movements and conduct regular and long-term training. Regarding supervisory work, in the past year, the members have mostly been unable to attend as scheduled due to concurrent positions, resulting in all work being trapped in a state of stagnation and decline. The audit of the funds of party headquarters in various places, the investigation of staff, the review of the government's policy guidelines, and the impeachment of derelict officials are all within their responsibilities, but they have not been fully implemented. Therefore, in the future, attention should be paid to the correction of the following items: (1) Strictly restrict those who do not attend the committee meetings. (2) Strictly implement the discipline of the party and promptly report those members and staff of party headquarters at all levels who abandon their responsibilities. (3) Closely supervise the government's policy guidelines and promptly impeach derelict officials. The above is a summary of the past year's party affairs in the city as a resolution on principles and methods. The fundamental spirit of the General Assembly in this resolution is to point out the various defects that have occurred in the past and to indicate the path for improvement in the future, so that party affairs can gradually develop from perfunctory to daily, and from coping to construction, so that the party's doctrine can gradually transition from speech to the realm of realization. This is the ambition that we hope all comrades in the city will work together to strive for and implement.

The purpose of the municipal report resolution of the Fifth Municipal Representative Assembly is to make Shanghai a model for the first city to complete the political tutelage work. Therefore, it pays equal attention to the construction undertakings during the political tutelage period and the training of the people to exercise political power. In the past year, the Shanghai Special Municipal Government has indeed made considerable progress in the construction undertakings during the political tutelage period, especially in the plan for the central urban area. The General Assembly is satisfied with this point and hopes for its early realization. However, the municipal government has not yet started to carry out the training of the people to exercise political power by district. Since the central government has determined the political tutelage period to be six years, the local governments should make preparations. The Sixth Municipal Representative Assembly has to solemnly point out that the municipal government needs to start training the people to use the four powers as soon as possible. It is hoped that starting from this year, the municipal government will effectively divide the area to train the people in preparation for the implementation of lower-level local self-government. All comrades in the city should also guide the people to accept training and promote all work related to local self-government based on the resolution of the Third Plenary Session, so as to cultivate the social foundation of local self-government. Then the goal of Shanghai as a model city that first completes the political tutelage work will not be in vain. Even in terms of the construction undertakings during the political tutelage period, although the municipal government has annually determined the policy guidelines and has gradually made progress, it still lacks an overall plan and steps due to the uncertainty of the political tutelage period in the past. In the future, it must be based on the work that should be completed during the political tutelage period as indicated in the Outline of National Construction, and aim to complete it in six years. It must be based on its own situation, and its annual progress steps. In short, "achieving the completion of political tutelage in six years" should be our only slogan and the only effort for the month in the future. Under this slogan of achieving the completion of political tutelage in six years, the responsibilities that the party and the government of this city should assume should be in compliance with the regulations of the central government without the need for further discussion. What the General Assembly particularly pays attention to is not how the party and the government should each be responsible, but how to seek the effective cooperation between the party and the government. The General Assembly believes that the work between the party and the government must echo each other, and the party and the government should exchange reports on their work and plans with each other within a certain period, so as to understand each other's facilities and prevent the progress of the political tutelage work from being hindered by the slight separation between the party and the government. Moreover, the party headquarters at the same level has the right to supervise the policy guidelines of the government at the same level, which has been clearly stipulated by the central government. Therefore, the policy guidelines of the municipal government and the laws and regulations that affect the rights and interests of citizens should be reviewed by the municipal party headquarters in advance. After all, the correction and remedy after the event are not as perfect as the consideration before the event. Moreover, when the household registration has not been completely cleared and the four powers have not been fully trained, the municipal party headquarters should truly represent the citizens and assume the responsibility of supervising the municipal government under the party's political tutelage. Therefore, the municipal party headquarters should fully exercise the functions of the Special Municipality Council as stipulated in Chapter 4 of the Special Municipality Organization Law before the citizens' right to vote can be legally exercised. This is what is hoped of the next

The Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committee should not easily abandon its responsibilities. The completion of the political tutelage work first lies in the richness of finance. The municipal government has indeed made progress in the consolidation of finance in the past year, so the income has also gradually increased, which is beneficial to the construction undertakings without saying anything. What the General Assembly believes should be reformed immediately is that the budget should be based on the previous year's final accounts as a considerable basis, and the actual future income and expenditure must also be roughly in line with it. If the actual income and expenditure are still inevitably chaotic, then the budget and final accounts are only similar to the report, which will inevitably affect the progress of various undertakings. Secondly, the tax revenue must gradually change from indirect tax to direct tax, especially the land tax, which is considered necessary to start levying as soon as possible. Regarding the collection of land tax, the measurement should be completed quickly first, but at a minimum, the land price should be started in the areas with prosperous household registration, such as Shanghai South, Zhabei, Yinxiang, and Yangjing, and the land tax should be implemented. In this way, the municipal government's financial income can be increased, and at the same time, the miscellaneous taxes should be reduced as much as possible to benefit democracy. Among other things, the most related to land administration is the deed system. The actual measurement bureau has now been received by the land bureau, and the deed has already started to be consolidated. However, since the land bureau has the regulations for issuing the land report deeds, the land outside the original concession area should never be issued deeds in the future. Among the deeds issued in the past, there are many cases of Chinese people using foreign merchants' names. The land bureau should also carefully plan methods to remove their names and reduce their effectiveness, so as not to lose the purpose of safeguarding land rights. Transportation undertakings are the most important in the political tutelage work. At present, this undertaking is subordinate to the Engineering, Public Utility, and Port Affairs Bureaus, which seems inevitable to be divided into their own administrations. Although the opening of roads has been determined to have a five-year plan, other transportation undertakings are still in progress without a plan, or are only in a position of supervision and guidance and cannot assume their responsibilities. In the future, a whole development plan and steps for the city's transportation should be determined first, and the progress should be mutually compatible with each other. Public security undertakings should aim to eliminate the obstacles to construction and all reactionary forces during the political tutelage period. Therefore, public security personnel should have a deep understanding of the party's doctrine. In the past year, the Public Security Bureau has failed to fulfill its responsibility to the party to eliminate reaction and protect the revolution. Therefore, the General Assembly believes that the Public Security Bureau should strive to improve so that it is not only a bureau of the municipal government to maintain law and order, but also an armed protection under the party's rule. In other words, all the forces of the Public Security Bureau must be used as an assistant to the implementation of the party's policies. Secondly, the police of the Public Security Bureau must be divided into traffic police, health police, and political police, and each should be given the knowledge and skills of the assigned duties so that they can fulfill their duties. Social undertakings should aim to realize the social policies of the party's principle of people's livelihood. The phenomenon of social poverty is increasing day by day, and the responsibilities of the Social Affairs Bureau will inevitably be heavier. In the past year, limited to the extremely small proportion of funds, the Social Affairs Bureau is still in the position of research, guidance, and supervision. However, social policies that are beneficial to the poor, rural areas, and consumers have gradually started their work, and the charity undertakings have also started to be consolidated. Unfortunately, the charity organizations are still controlled by a small number of good sticks. Although there are one or two more sensible and impartial people, they cannot save it. The Social Affairs Bureau has not been able to vigorously implement the resolution of the Fifth Municipal Representative Assembly and fight against the local bullies. The General Assembly cannot but feel disappointed. Therefore, the General Assembly believes that the funds for social undertakings should be increased in the future so that there will be opportunities for considerable development. At the same time, the Social Affairs Bureau should be urged to hold a thorough disinfection work for the corrupt charity organizations with a fearless spirit. Health undertakings are extremely important to the health of citizens. In the past year, the Health Bureau has been working hard in school health and epidemic prevention. However, the unclean streets are still eye-catching, and the instructions to citizens on health knowledge are also insufficient. In the future, it should cooperate effectively with the party headquarters and carry out regular health movements as stipulated by the central government so that citizens know the importance and methods of health. Then everything related to health undertakings can be properly arranged. Education undertakings are extremely important to the training of the people to exercise political power. Although the city's education funds have increased today, its percentage has dropped from 25% to 19.77%, which has to arouse the serious attention of the General Assembly. With the majority of the city's school-age children out of school and the large number of adult illiterates, the education funds must maintain its ratio of 25% at least, and then we can expect the popularization of education. The General Assembly believes that the purpose of vigorously implementing the education of the Three Principles of the People is not only to instill the party's doctrine, but also to cultivate the backbone elements to save the decline of the nation. Therefore, school education must make students understand the position of the Chinese nation and the necessity of saving methods, the Three Principles of the People, cultivate their spirit of fighting for survival for the nation, and be able to fight for the nation's physical strength. All those who slightly involve the meaning of decadence and romance should be vigorously cleared up. Adult education should cooperate with the party headquarters in the future and make full efforts to eradicate illiteracy within the six-year period of political tutelage. In addition, such as the fact that education funds must not be misappropriated and the raising of education funds are the current important plans. The unification of the city's education rights is also considered necessary to be realized immediately. The realization of the central urban area plan should be an important task for us in the future. This work requires the government's strict plan and effective implementation, and especially requires close cooperation with the party. The General Assembly specially indicates that this plan is the real foundation for Shanghai to get rid of imperialist rule. Therefore, all comrades in the city must work together, cooperate with the government, and fight together to the end.

▲ Resolution on the Report of the Garrison Work: After listening to the report of the Songhu Garrison Command on the garrison work, the General Assembly knew that there was no negligence in the city's defense in the past year, the law and order was gradually consolidated, the intelligence could be valued, and the construction of military industry could also be carried out according to the opportunity. I feel satisfied. However, this city is the area where imperialism is the most rampant, and it is also the base camp for all reactionary elements to conspire to make trouble. The General Assembly deeply knows that the reactionary elements have not weakened their delusion of rebellion because they are attached to imperialism, and imperialism also uses the hands of reactionary elements to increase its means of bullying. In order to maintain the safety of the rear and consolidate the national foundation,

The resolution is as follows: (1) The city is vast, and the police force is slightly weak. In addition, all the rebellious people gather here. Without considerable troops, the occurrence of danger is inevitable. Therefore, the Fifth Division of the garrison in this city should be temporarily suspended from other transfers unless there is a special need. The garrison commander should also base on the importance of the defense zone to determine the deployment of soldiers throughout the city. (2) The number of reactionary elements hiding in this city is not small, but the number of good citizens is more than ten thousand times greater. If the good citizens can unite as one, no matter how cunning and cunning the reactionaries are, they will never be able to achieve their goals. Unfortunately, the citizens' knowledge is insufficient and the unity is weak. Therefore, in order to strictly prevent the conspiracy of the reactionaries to wantonly disrupt, the declaration of temporary martial law is not necessarily an appropriate measure. However, the implementation of martial law is often not announced, causing young children and weak women to sleep in the deep night. This point should be paid attention to. Moreover, after martial law, there must be a lifting of martial law, but only continuous martial law is heard, and there is no news of the lifting of martial law, causing the general public to be in a state of danger and fear every day. The commercial sector is particularly affected. In the future, for martial law, unless it is very urgent or contains a time limit, it should be announced in advance so that the public knows. The usual martial law should only be implemented for inspection and should be lifted by order on the day of the stability of the situation to reassure the public. (2) At this time of national crisis, the Communist Party has not been completely eliminated, and most of the reactionary factions have not disappeared. In addition, the bandits in the counties along the Yangtze River are rampant, and the people are in dire straits. The Garrison Command should prepare to completely eliminate all reactionary forces with most of its strength. Even if there are those who hide in the concession and are sheltered by imperialism, the Garrison Command should also properly deal with them so that they do not escape the net. The General Assembly is also very willing to provide strong assistance to the Garrison Command in this regard. (4) The most important part of the pacification work is the collection of intelligence. However, after the intelligence is collected, it should be immediately tracked down and the case should be solved. In the past, our party headquarters also cooperated in the intelligence work, but after the case was solved, it was found that some of the criminals were released on bail due to insufficient evidence, and some were allowed to roam free because the bailor was more powerful. The General Assembly sincerely hopes that the Garrison Command can deal with all the rebels who attempt to subvert the party and the country with the spirit of revolution and not tolerate them in the slightest, so that the comrades will not suffer great misfortune. (5) There has been no report from the Garrison Commander on the banning of newspapers and the inspection of mail related to the pacification. The General Assembly deeply knows that the Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Headquarters has cooperated with the Garrison Command with the greatest efforts, and the results are considerable. However, this kind of ban is only a last resort, and the Garrison Commander should be asked to handle it with extreme caution. The General Assembly is also willing to urge the Propaganda Department of the Municipal Party Headquarters to pay attention to the efforts and assist with all their heart. (6) Due to military influences in the past year, the work of military industry and road construction has not been implemented. The General Assembly regrets this very much. The Prime Minister's military industry policy should be vigorously implemented by those who are currently in charge of military affairs. In the past, it was too urgent to defend, and there was no time to carry it out. In the future, attention should be paid to this. If it cannot be held due to insufficient funds, the General Assembly is very willing to arouse the public with the greatest efforts and assist with all their heart so that the work of road construction can be completed and the Prime Minister's instructions can be realized. (7) The construction of barracks is especially needed. It is not appropriate for the army to occupy civilian houses in terms of discipline, and it is not elegant in terms of appearance. Qian Dajun, the former commander of the Songhu Garrison, once raised huge sums of money from all parties, but nothing has been done. The General Assembly has not heard any reports from the current commander, which is really doubtful. The Garrison Command should be asked to investigate the case and urge its implementation.

American Minister Johnson Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday Morning 102

He Will Return to Beijing Next Wednesday

A Banquet Held by the American Chamber of Commerce Last Night

American Minister to China, Mr. Johnson, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning after traveling from Beiping to Beijing for negotiations on outstanding Sino-American issues. He had also attended banquets hosted by National Government Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, Legislative Yuan President Hu Hanmin, and Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting during his two-week stay in Beijing. He is currently residing at the American Club and plans to stay in Shanghai for approximately one week before returning to Beijing next Wednesday to continue negotiations on the outstanding Sino-American issues. It is also reported that the Sino-American aviation contract will also be negotiated and revised by Minister Johnson.

Minister Johnson's Remarks: Our reporter visited Minister Johnson at the American Club yesterday, and the conversation was mainly about miscellaneous matters and did not touch upon diplomatic issues. Minister Johnson mentioned that his journey from Beiping to Beijing via the Blue Jinpu Train was peaceful. His time in Beijing was also calm and normal, but recent telegram exchanges have led to more rumors. There were reports of disruptions on the Jinpu Railway near Dezhou, but the actual situation is not as severe as reported. He is scheduled to return to Beijing on the 12th of this month. At this point, Mr. Deng Bi, the Second Secretary of the American Embassy who had accompanied the Minister on his trip south, entered the room. Minister Johnson introduced him to the reporter, stating that Mr. Deng Bi was born in Beiping, his father had served as the Consul-General in Shanghai, and his grandfather had been the Minister to China. Thus, three generations of his family have been in China, and under the principle of territoriality, Mr. Deng Bi is practically a Chinese person.

Banquet by the American Club: The American Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai had originally planned to host a banquet to welcome Minister Johnson upon his arrival in China at the beginning of February. However, the banquet was postponed because the Minister had to wait until he had formally presented his credentials to the National Government before accepting private banquets. The banquet was finally held last night at the American Club, attended by American expatriates. The attendees included Minister Johnson, Embassy Secretary Deng Bi, Consul-General Cunningham, Attorney General Pandi, Commander of the Yangtze River Fleet Craven, Director-General of the Municipal Council Fessenden, Princeton University Professor Gibbons, and President of St. John's University Bu Fangji, among over two hundred others. At the end of the banquet, American Chamber of Commerce President Raven delivered a welcoming speech, Consul-General Cunningham gave an introductory speech, and Minister Johnson delivered a brief thank-you speech, expressing his hope for sincere cooperation between China and the United States before the event concluded. The United China Association is also scheduled to host a public banquet this afternoon.

Attitudes of Various Countries Towards China's New Tariff Schedule 105

Separate "Expert Commissioners" Will Be Appointed for Discussion

The national new tariff schedule drafted by the Tariff Commission had been pre-approved by Foreign Minister Wang with various countries. However, due to the delay in the signing of the new treaty with Japan, it has not been formally announced to this day. Yesterday, it was learned that the detailed rules on reciprocal tariffs and commodity classification will be discussed by a meeting of expert commissioners separately appointed by various countries. Japan has decided to appoint Finance Official Komori Tairo as the expert commissioner to jointly negotiate with the Japanese Charge d'Affaires Shigemitsu Aoi. Once formally agreed, a protocol will be signed, and the new tariff schedule will be announced and implemented before the Sino-Japanese revision of the new treaty.

Japan Denies Sending Troops to Shandong 106

Shigemitsu Aoi to Go to Beijing Next Week

Japanese Consul-General in Shanghai, Shigemitsu Aoi, who had been ill for several days, finally met with Japanese newspaper reporters yesterday. It was reported that Shigemitsu stated that after news reports alleged that Japanese residents in Jinan telegraphed the Tokyo government requesting troops to be sent to Shandong, he immediately telegraphed his home government to inquire about the matter. He was completely denied the Jinan Japanese Resident's request for troops. The Japanese government also has no intention of sending troops to Shandong again. Shigemitsu continued that the Sino-Japanese tariff protocol is currently in negotiations on specific issues, and he is scheduled to go to Beijing within the next week.

County Government Prepares for Price Stabilization of Rice 107

Issuing Money Instead of Grain

Recently, Shanghai County Magistrate Leng, due to the ever-increasing price of rice, making it difficult for people to afford food, it is urgent to provide relief. A special letter was sent to the Property Management Office to find ways to organize price stabilization of rice. After the office convened a meeting of district chiefs, it was unanimously agreed that purchasing and transporting rice to open price stabilization would not only involve complicated procedures but also be difficult to implement universally. It was decided to follow the methods of the Republic of China Year 9, issuing money instead of grain. Each district would investigate poor households within its jurisdiction and issue funds accordingly. The office has recorded the case and sent a letter to the county government for approval.

Port Authority Regulates Vessels Traveling to and from Yujidun 108

The section of the river channel downstream from the Wusongkou Yujidun has been poorly maintained for years and is severely silted up, causing vessels to run aground frequently. The Port Authority has been planning to dredge the channel, but fearing that this will not be enough to solve the problem quickly, it has formulated regulations for traffic and has consulted with the Public Security Bureau to set up a water patrol team stationed at Panlonggang Yujidun to provide immediate assistance. The proposed regulations and budget for the water patrol team have been approved by the municipal government. Currently, the ten articles of the regulations are being jointly issued by the Port Authority and the Public Security Bureau to ensure that vessels traveling in the area do not run aground again.

First Phase Results of the Cotton Planting Cooperative Area 109

Highest Production Reaches 169 Jin Per Mu

The Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs, recognizing that the cotton planting area in each district of this city accounts for more than 40%, and that the selection of varieties and cultivation methods are all conventional and unimproved, resulting in a year-by-year decline in cotton production, which is detrimental to the livelihood of citizens, initiated a cotton planting cooperative experiment last year. Seeds and fertilizers were provided by the Bureau, and a subsidy of five yuan per mu was also provided. The experiment was first conducted in six districts of the Lixing District of Pudong, and the results were satisfactory. The per-mu production of cooperative farmers in the district reached over 169 jin for Chen Zhuoyun and Hu Ansheng, and over 125 jin for Ji Langqing and Xu Guiting. It is now reported that the Bureau has approved the issuance of certificates of commendation to encourage them. The grading of awards is temporarily divided into three types: (1) those who harvest 100 jin or more of cotton per mu will be given a Class C certificate; (2) those who harvest 125 jin or more will be given a Class B certificate; (3) those who harvest 150 jin or more will be given a Class A certificate. In the future, if there is any special production, those who reach 200 jin or more per mu will be given a special certificate.

Commodity Inspection Bureau Encourages Silk Merchants 110

Regarding the inspection of exported raw silk, silk merchants requested an extension because they needed time to prepare to adopt the public weight system. In order to consider the difficulties of merchants and maintain credibility, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce decided that the newly revised detailed rules would be implemented from March 1st, but the inspection of export quantities would be temporarily exempted until April 1st. The Bureau felt that although this issue has been resolved, it was deeply concerned that the silk merchants may still not understand the true facts and still have many doubts. Therefore, it sent separate letters to the silk factory associations and silk factories, explaining the situation in detail and inviting them to the Bureau to visit, study, and test the various inspections of raw silk, so that they can understand the facts and dispel their doubts. The original letter is recorded as follows:

Attached Original Letter: Respectfully, our Bureau is entrusted by the Ministry to handle inspection affairs. Its sole purpose is to assist merchants in improving commodities so that foreign trade will develop day by day. To achieve this goal, the strength of the government, the knowledge of scholars, and the experience of merchants must be combined into one. Therefore, for the establishment of each inspection office, specialized scholars must be invited as directors and technicians, and industry leaders must be invited as deputy directors and consultants. The hope of implementing government-merchant cooperation is that the intended goals can eventually be achieved. Last year, when preparing to establish the Raw Silk Inspection Office, the Bureau submitted a request to the Ministry to appoint industry leaders Huang Chen, Shen Huachen, Chen Haoquan, Cheng Bingruo, Wu Shenbo, Li Youren, and silk industry experts Miao Zhongxiu and Zhou Yanding as preparatory committee members. After the preparation was completed, Miao Zhongxiu was invited to be the director, Huang Chengzhi was invited to be the deputy director, and Lan En, Li Dizhong, and Guo Limao were invited to be technicians. All equipment, except for a portion accepted from the former International Raw Silk Inspection Institute, was purchased from Germany, Switzerland, the United States, and Japan at a cost of approximately 200,000 yuan, so that Chinese and foreign silk merchants can be satisfied at the time of opening. During the drafting of the detailed rules for raw silk inspection, a total of 14 preparatory committee meetings were held, and it was considered for a long period of ten months that the public weight system would not cause any losses to both parties in the transaction, and the trade behavior was the most fair. Japan had already implemented this system two years ago, and European silk-producing countries also use the public weight system for exported raw silk. The world trend has been consistent. Some may worry that the silk body will be damaged and the seller will suffer losses when taking public weight, but according to the many years of inspection experience of the former International Raw Silk Inspection Institute, taking public weight does not damage the silk body, and the over-dried strips or fictitious damages can still be used, so it was decided to adopt the public weight system to follow the trend and avoid falling behind. After the Ministry promulgated this system, it was originally scheduled to be implemented on February 1st. Later, your industry representatives requested an extension because the valuation of raw silk sales and purchases must also be reformed, and everything must be prepared, and the Ministry approved an extension of one month. Unexpectedly, after the expiration of the period, your industry representatives still stated that the procedures for public weight sales and purchases were not yet ready, and some silk merchants did not yet understand the advantages of the public weight system, and requested another extension. The Ministry believed that the business situation must be considered, but credibility should also be maintained, and repeated extensions were not appropriate. Therefore, it was decided that the newly revised detailed rules would still be implemented from March 1st, but the inspection of export quantities would be temporarily exempted until April 1st, and exemption certificates would be issued for export. Now that the issue of public weight inspection has been resolved, and all equipment in our Bureau's Raw Silk Inspection Office has been arranged, if you are willing to come to the Bureau for a practical visit and study of the various inspections of raw silk, please come to the Raw Silk Inspection Office between 3:00 PM and 5:00 PM every day from March 10th to March 20th. Our Bureau will order the staff of the office to put aside all matters and sincerely wait for your visit to explain everything. If you can bring silk samples to the Bureau for testing, so as to dispel all doubts with facts and jointly promote the progress of foreign trade in raw silk, it would be especially welcomed. I hereby inform you, and hope you will investigate. Best regards, Zou Bingwen, Director of Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, March 6th, 19th Year [of the Republic].

Ministry of Finance Issues Awards for Fundraising Encouragement 112

The Bond Solicitation Committee of the Ministry of Finance sent a letter yesterday to the wealthy individuals and commercial organizations in Shanghai that actively responded to the bond solicitation, stating, in summary, that the committee had previously reported to the Ministry the list of those who actively subscribed to the various bonds issued by the Ministry of Finance. The Ministry of Finance has now replied that the award-winning households have been reviewed in accordance with the Ministry's Bond Award Regulations and Detailed Rules for Implementation. Chairman of the Municipal Council, Arnold, Resigns 114

Shanghai Times reported that the current Chairman of the Municipal Council, Arnold, submitted his resignation at yesterday's (5th) board meeting and retired on the same day. It is said that Arnold's resignation was probably due to the results of this election. In addition to preparing the administrative report for the year, the old board of directors is required to prepare the budget for the coming year, which is submitted to the taxpayers' meeting for approval, and then implemented by the new board of directors. Arnold is the chairman, but he will not be on the board next time, and he feels that there are difficulties in fulfilling the duties of preparing the budget, so he resigned.

Japanese Aircraft Still Did Not Arrive in Shanghai Yesterday 115

The regular aviation route of the Japan Aviation Transport Company from Najima, Fukuoka to Shanghai was originally scheduled to have a test flight on the 5th of this month, but was changed to fly to Shanghai on the morning of yesterday (the 6th) due to a hurricane and was expected to arrive in the afternoon. Holidays for Factory Workers 116

The municipal government approved the consultation from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce yesterday, in accordance with the instructions from the Executive Yuan, regarding the regulations on holidays for factory workers. The 70th Central Standing Committee meeting decided that the factory's annual shutdown dates should be in accordance with the regulations for single anniversary memorial services, which are January 1st, March 12th, March 29th, July 9th, October 10th, November 12th, and add May 1st, Labor Day, for a total of seven days. The method of paying wages for workers on Sundays should be handled in accordance with legally valid collective consultations or work contracts. If there is no consultation contract, it should be determined according to whether the work is long-term or short-term, etc. The municipal government has instructed the Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs to inform them.

If your office has burned soil, please promptly fill in and send the photos and quantity of poison destruction to the association for compilation. The number of people who sent the association to the association in the past was very large, and the association has started to sort out and compile a panorama of poison destruction, which will be published soon.

The First District Office of Shanghai County held its eighth district affairs meeting yesterday.
